The Ubuntu Code of Conduct

Launchpad users can sign the Ubuntu Code of Conduct. The list of Ubunteros can be found below.

The Ubuntero List

The individual and/or entities names listed below have signed the Ubuntu Code of Conduct.

For tracking / identifying persons (if Signed Ubuntu Code of Conduct says Yes) the posted format is: contributor name – Launchpad usernames.
